[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2220[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_offset == offset + linelen + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m && len >= [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2221[0m[39m:      [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2222[0m[39m:       * Well, we saw a one-character line ending, so either it's a CR[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2223[0m[39m:       * or an LF; we have at least two characters left, including the[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2224[0m[39m:       * CR.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2225[0m[39m:       *[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2226[0m[39m:       * If the line ending is a CR, skip all subsequent CRs; at[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2227[0m[39m:       * least one capture appeared to have multiple CRs at the end of[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2228[0m[39m:       * a line.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2229[0m[39m:       *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2230[0m[39m:      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset + linelen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[32m'\r'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2231[0m[39m:        last_char_was_cr = true;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2232[0m[39m:        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && [0m[1;35mtvb_offset_exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, next_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2233[0m[39m:          c = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, next_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2234[0m[39m:          next_offset++;        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* skip over that character *[0m[35m/[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2235[0m[39m:          len--;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2236[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'\n'[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m && last_char_was_cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2237[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2238[0m[39m:             * LF is a line ending, whether preceded by CR or not.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2239[0m[39m:             * NUL is a line ending if preceded by CR.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2240[0m[39m:             *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2241[0m[39m:            break;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2242[0m[39m:          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2243[0m[39m:          last_char_was_cr = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'\r'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2244[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2245[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2246[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2247[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2248[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2249[0m[39m:     * Now compute the length of the line *including* the end-of-line[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2250[0m[39m:     * indication, if any; we display it all.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2198[0m[39m:  while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && [0m[1;35mtvb_offset_exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2199[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2200[0m[39m:     * Find the end of the line.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2201[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2202[0m[39m:    linelen = [0m[1;35mtvb_find_line_end[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, len, &next_offset, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2203[0m[39m:    len -= next_offset - offset;        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* subtract out the line's characters [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2204[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2205[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Telnet RFC [0m[1;36m1184[0m[39m allows for specifying window size via columns and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheight.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2206[0m[39m:       If this subopt is set then a method for storing the data in a given [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwindow[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2207[0m[39m:       is necessary.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2208[0m[39m:    *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2209[0m[39m:   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2210[0m[39m:    int start_offset = hf_telnet_width * hf_telnet_line;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2211[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mtvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinelen < hf_telnet_width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlinelen : hf_telnet_width, hf_naws_data + start_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2212[0m[39m:    hf_telnet_line = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_line + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m % hf_telnet_height;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2213[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:636[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m643[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m636:d[0m[1;35missect_linemode_subopt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_info *pinfo, const char *optname _U_, tvbuff_t [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*tvb _U_, int offset _U_,[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m637[0m[39m:                    int len _U_, proto_tree *tree _U_, proto_item *item _U_[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m638[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m639[0m[39m:  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set [0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m640[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m641[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m642[0m[39m:  return;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m643[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The AddressSanitizer report shows that the global buffer `hf_naws_data`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated by `dissect_naws_subopt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `wmem_alloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, is later freed prematurely [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `dissect_linemode_subopt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `wmem_free`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without resetting the associated [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“active” flag `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set`. After the free, further text processing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `telnet_add_text` still sees `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set == [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` and performs a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, hf_naws_data + start_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, causing a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse-after-free write into the freed region.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic Preservation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The NAWS sub-option functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mallocating a buffer to hold rows of text, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mkeeping track of width/height/line[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain intact.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory for `hf_naws_data` should continue to belong to the Wireshark packet [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory-pool [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`pinfo->pool`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and be freed appropriately [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto avoid unbounded growth [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif multiple NAWS suboptions appear[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other sub-options [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., COMPORT, AUTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and all existing tests/harness code [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust be unaffected.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In dissect_linemode_subopt [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `packet-telnet.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, after freeing [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`hf_naws_data`, clear both the “active” flag and the pointer to avoid stale [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Specifically, change:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          hf_naws_data = NULL;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. No changes are needed in `telnet_add_text`; clearing the flag prevents that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction from entering the NAWS buffer‐write branch when the buffer has been freed.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effect Analysis  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By zeroing out `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set`, we ensure that `telnet_add_text`’s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be false whenever the buffer has been[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed, thus eliminating the use-after-free.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Nullifying `hf_naws_data` adds an extra safety measure; even if code elsewhere[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merroneously checks the pointer rather than the flag, it will encounter a NULL.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change preserves the allocation/free pattern: new NAWS sub-options will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill allocate a fresh buffer and set the flag, and a linemode sub-option will [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests and fuzz harness logic are unchanged; only the lifetime state [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the NAWS buffer is corrected.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
